Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# HTTP GET with bounded exponential-backoff retry on transient 5xx responses.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# On any non-5xx response (including auth errors), populates z_code_file and returns.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# On curl-network failure or exhausted 5xx retries, buc_die. The caller evaluates
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# the final HTTP status via its own case-switch on the populated z_code_file.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# Extract '.error.message' from a JSON response file for diagnostic surfacing.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# Returns a fallback string for empty/missing/malformed bodies. jq stderr captured
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# to the paired stderr file (no suppression). Exactly one line printed in all paths.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  jq -e . "${z_resp_file}" > /dev/null 2>>"${z_stderr_file}" \
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  jq -r '.error.message // "no error.message field"' "${z_resp_file}" 2>>"${z_stderr_file}" \
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# Execute one Artifact Registry packages.list probe call for a JWT SA role.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# and prints the resulting HTTP code to stdout. Verdict logic lives in the caller
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# fail-fast on other shapes. buc_dies only on infrastructure failures.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "Build Artifact Registry packages.list URL"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "Call Artifact Registry packages.list (with transient-5xx retry)"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "AR packages.list HTTP ${z_code} for role ${z_role} attempt ${z_attempt}"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# Execute one CRM projects.get probe iteration for the Payor OAuth flow.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# and stderr to ZRBGV_CRM_STDERR_FILE (kindle-constant paths for forensic visibility).
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "Build CRM projects.get URL"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "Call CRM projects.get on payor project (with transient-5xx retry)"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_log_args "CRM projects.get HTTP ${z_code} for Payor iteration ${z_iteration}"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:      if jq -e . "${ZRBGV_CRM_RESP_FILE}" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:        z_err=$(jq -r '.error.message // "Unknown error"' "${ZRBGV_CRM_RESP_FILE}" 2>/dev/null) || z_err="Unknown error"
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# Bounded propagation-absorbing retry. First HTTP 200/206 wins; HTTP 403 (the
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# any other HTTP code dies with body summary. Past max attempts on 403, dies with
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# body summary as 'budget exhausted'. Layers cleanly with rbgo_get_token_capture's
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:# JWT-signature retry: each layer recognizes its own 'not yet' and retries.
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:#   1. Authenticate via zrbgp_authenticate_capture (RBRO refresh token -> access token)
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:#   2. Call CRM projects.get on payor project to verify token works
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:#   3. Sleep for configured delay
Tools/rbk/rbgv_AccessProbe.sh:  buc_doc_brief "Probe Payor OAuth access against Cloud Resource Manager (CRM) projects.get"

Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # the store to the file store. At this Pale (docker's own credential store,
Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # store itself (the config.json `auths` map docker push reads directly — the
Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # form WSL uses natively) and treats login as done. A real auth failure emits
Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # "unauthorized" and never matches. Stable Win32 system-error message;
Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # corroborated by docker/cli#4353 and #1263. REMOVE the bend when the
Tools/rbk/rbgc_Constants.sh:  # uncontrolled-Cygwin host gains an interactive Windows logon / working vault.

Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   identity. There are no concurrent writers in the same project.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   is pristine for the resources they manage. If a resource "already exists"
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   (HTTP 409), that's treated as state drift or prior manual activity.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# - Policy: All HTTP 409 Conflict responses are fatal (buc_die). We do not
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   treat 409 as idempotent success anywhere in RBGI.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   If you see a 409, resolve state drift first (destroy/reset), then rerun.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   (a) Resource creation: "already exists" — state drift or prior manual activity.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   (b) setIamPolicy: "ABORTED" — etag mismatch from concurrent policy change.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   Both are fatal under single-writer invariant. Google-internal auto-provisioning
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:#   can trigger (b) outside our control; the 409 surfaces a real concurrency issue.

Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Revoke (member removal) — inverse of the add_*_iam_role trio.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# APIs with distinct getIamPolicy/setIamPolicy shapes (BCG load-bearing). They
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# share only the jq member-removal transform.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Leaner than the add trio, but not class-free. The member being revoked is
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# exist" / backward "is not deleted") cannot fire on a revoke and are dropped.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# propagated its roles/owner to the resource-scope IAM cache. So the
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# empowerment instantly). setIamPolicy stays lean: it is gated by the same
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# 409 stays fatal under the single-writer invariant, transient 5xx retried.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Removing an absent member is a jq no-op, so revoke is idempotent. Fatal on
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# failure like every regular function — divest calls them as ordinary commands.

Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# to ensure consistent conditional role binding support across Google Cloud APIs.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# This is enforced by default in all policy operations to prevent version drift.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      .version = 3 |
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      .bindings = (.bindings // []) |
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      if ([.bindings[]? | .role] | index($role))
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      then .bindings |= map(if .role == $role
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:                            then .members = ((.members // []) + [$member] | unique)
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:                            else . end)
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      else .bindings += [{role: $role, members: [$member]}]
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      | (if $etag != "" then .etag = $etag else . end)
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# rbgi_jq_add_member_to_role_capture. This is the one legitimate shared helper
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# scope). jq subtraction drops all occurrences of the member, so an absent
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# member is a no-op (idempotent). A binding left with no members is pruned —
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# since other bindings are untouched and arrive non-empty from getIamPolicy.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      .version = 3 |
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      .bindings = (.bindings // []) |
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      .bindings |= ( map(if .role == $role
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:                         then .members = ((.members // []) - [$member])
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:                         else . end)
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:                     | map(select((.members // []) | length > 0)) )
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:      | (if $etag != "" then .etag = $etag else . end)
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Provision service agent (Google-managed service account) for an enabled API.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Uses serviceusage.googleapis.com generateServiceIdentity to deterministically
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# ensure the service agent exists before granting it IAM roles.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:# Prints the service agent email to stdout.
Tools/rbk/rbgi_IAM.sh:  local -r z_url="https://serviceusage.googleapis.com/v1beta1/projects/${z_project_id}/services/${z_api_service}.googleapis.com:generateServiceIdentity"

Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:#     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# limitations under the License.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Author: Brad Hyslop <bhyslop@scaleinvariant.org>
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# kind. Takes a recipe (ordered, pre-resolved step rows) plus an opaque
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# step's buildStepOutputs slot. Owns NO kind knowledge: the recipe and the
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# passed by the body. Capture-domain constants (the mason capture SA, the TETHER
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# a per-kind choice. Built on the rbfcb_ build primitives (write-script-body,
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# wait-build-completion), which it calls rather than absorbs.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Contract: RBSCJ "Capture Composition Contract".
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Internal: dispatch-time substitution-coverage check. A capture step reads
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# to surface (it costs the whole cook). The _RBGL_* references in a step body ARE
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# register. Sentinel-free return-1 primitive, like the rbfcb_ build primitives the
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# dispatch loop already rides; the caller buc_die's with the step identity.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# inter-step channel keeps its own in-step guards and is out of scope.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  # Keys as newline-bounded text for builtin whole-line membership tests. Empty
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  # keys (a blob declaring no registers) is legitimate — no test -n.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  # Load the body, then iterate — the file is closed before the scan begins.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    # documentation, not a read; a trailing inline mention stays conservative.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    # the next token on the line surfaces.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# plus an opaque substitutions blob.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Build envelope's `substitutions` field; the spine reads no key from it. The
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# envelope shape (serviceAccount, options.automapSubstitutions, options.logging,
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# options.pool, timeout) is the spine's; the values that vary by capture domain
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# (mason SA, TETHER pool, regime timeout) are spine-owned constants.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# Args: token label poll_ceiling subs_file temp_prefix recipe_row...
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  # already include-expanded (zrbld_spine_validate). A JSON object cannot carry
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  # duplicate keys, so no dedup is needed.
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  local -r z_keys_file="${z_temp_prefix}subs_keys.txt"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  local -r z_steps_file="${z_temp_prefix}steps.json"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    z_body_file="${z_temp_prefix}${z_id}_body.txt"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    z_escaped_file="${z_temp_prefix}${z_id}_escaped.txt"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    z_steps_built="${z_temp_prefix}${z_id}_steps.json"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:      '. + [{name: $name, id: $id, script: $script}]' \
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  local -r z_build_file="${z_temp_prefix}build.json"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  z_build_id=$(rbuh_json_field_capture "lode_build_create" '.metadata.build.id') \
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:    || buc_die "Failed to capture build ID from builds.create response"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  test -n "${z_build_id}" || buc_die "Build ID empty in builds.create response"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# slot into a destination file. The step index is the only generic parameter;
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# knowledge, not the spine's. Reads ZRBFC_BUILD_STATUS_FILE (the terminal build
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:# result registered by zrbfc_wait_build_completion).
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  local -r z_b64_file="${z_dest_file}.b64"
Tools/rbk/rblds_Spine.sh:  jq -r ".results.buildStepOutputs[${z_step_index}] // empty" "${ZRBFC_BUILD_STATUS_FILE}" \

Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:# to Cloud Build. Checks two layers in dependency order:
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:#   1. Reliquary — co-versioned builder tool images (gcloud, docker, syft, etc.)
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:#      created by inscribe. One reliquary per depot setup. Enshrine depends on it.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:#   2. Enshrine — upstream base images copied into private GAR, pinned by content
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:#      hash. One enshrine per base image anchor. Multiple vessels sharing the same
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:#      anchor only need one enshrine.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:# A missing image at either layer causes a Cloud Build failure minutes later.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:# This preflight catches it immediately with copy-paste remediation commands.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:# and authentication (needs token for registry API).
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:  # RBRV_IMAGE_n_ANCHOR (locator: package-path:tag). Enshrine copies the upstream
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:  # image into the enshrine namespace, pinned by content hash. The conjure
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:  # Dockerfile's FROM references the locator-resolved GAR ref, not upstream tag.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    # Skip slots without an origin (no base image to enshrine).
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    # Anchor handling depends on egress mode. Tether passes through (buildx
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    # fetches upstream at build time). Airgap requires a populated anchor
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    # a non-empty origin guarantees runtime build failure.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:        # repo). Discriminate by whether origin resolves to a vessel directory.
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "  ${z_anchor_var} is a hallmark-pin, not an enshrine locator — enshrine is not invoked on this vessel."
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "  Ordain the producer vessel first, then write its hallmark into ${z_anchor_var}."
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "    # in ${z_vessel_dir}/rbrv.env, then:"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "  Airgap conjure cannot reach upstream — base images must be enshrined first."
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "  The anchor locator points at the enshrined image inside GAR. Without it,"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:          buc_bare "  the airgap worker pool has no source for the base image and the build fails."
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    z_status_file="${ZRBFD_PREFLIGHT_PREFIX}enshrine_${z_n}_status.txt"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    z_response_file="${ZRBFD_PREFLIGHT_PREFIX}enshrine_${z_n}_response.txt"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:    z_stderr_file="${ZRBFD_PREFLIGHT_PREFIX}enshrine_${z_n}_stderr.txt"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:      buc_bare "  Enshrine copies upstream base images (e.g., busybox:latest from Docker Hub) into"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:      buc_bare "  your private GAR, pinned by content hash. Like the reliquary, this ensures"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:      buc_bare "  air-gapped builds never reach the public internet. The anchor locator is stable"
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:      buc_bare "  until you deliberately re-enshrine to pick up a newer upstream version."
Tools/rbk/rbfd_FoundryDirectorBuild.sh:      buc_bare "  Multiple vessels sharing the same base image anchor need only one enshrine."

Tools/rbk/rbuh_Http.sh:# recreate. GCP IAM's SA read path is multi-replica eventually-consistent: a
Tools/rbk/rbuh_Http.sh:# fail-loud on a stale read. Requiring consecutive 404s debounces that flap; any

Tools/rbk/rbuh_Http.sh:# RBGC_MAX_CONSISTENCY_SEC.

Tools/rbk/rbgp_Payor.sh:# projectId (everything before the "-d-" infix). Consumers walking by
Tools/rbk/rbgp_Payor.sh:# depots walk all subdirs.

Tools/rbk/rbgp_Payor.sh:# displayName does not parse to a valid RBRR-canonical moniker are skipped.

Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# Implements the depot-immutable tripwire. At end of successful levy
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# the Payor inscribes a FROM-scratch image carrying rbmm_moorings/rbrd.env to
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# GAR at rbi_df/rbrd:tripwire. Every cloud-submitting command pulls
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# post-levy hand-edit of rbrd.env dies loudly instead of silently
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# differing from the depot's worker-pool quotas, region, and identity.
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# (bespoke implementation). See CLAUDE.md "Prefix Naming Discipline".

Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:  # Shape: <region>-docker.pkg.dev/<depot-project>/<gar-repo>/rbi_df/rbrd:tripwire
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# using a bearer token. Idempotent — repeated calls refresh credential.
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# shares only the signature + retry-budget constants out of rbgc. Real auth
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# failures do not match the signature and fail fast.
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# Inscribe the tripwire image at end of successful levy.
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# inscribed; must be unmade and relevied to refresh).
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# param1 channel). The former is the consuming-CLI path (caller has a
Tools/rbk/rbndb_base.sh:# token in scope); the latter is the rbw-rdi tabtarget path.

Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # shared library snippet (requires ORIGIN + RAW_FILE; provides SHA + FINGERPRINT).
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  RAW_FILE="/workspace/ensconce_raw_${SLOT}.json"
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # Collision guard — never silently clobber an existing Lode. The bole handle
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # absent => a fresh touchmark; present => re-use. Re-use is legitimate ONLY when
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # bytes); a different digest under the same touchmark is a clobber and fails loud.
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # GAR write in the sense the spec requires (no host pre-submit window). EXISTING_SHA
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # apples-to-apples. An inspect failure is treated as absent: cloud-side auth/network
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # is reliable, and a genuine GAR outage fails the copy below regardless.
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  EXISTING_RAW="/workspace/ensconce_existing_${SLOT}.json"
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:      echo "Touchmark ${STAMP} already holds identical digest sha256:${SHA} — idempotent retry, proceeding."
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:    echo "Touchmark ${STAMP} is fresh (no existing :${_RBGL_TAG_BOLE})."
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # Copy upstream into the Lode package under the canonical digest tag.
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # Apply remaining member tags by GAR->GAR retag (same blobs, manifest re-tag only).
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # host capture-file). No jq dependency — values are controlled (sanitized origin,
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # hex digest, SA email, build id, ISO timestamp); none can carry a literal quote.
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # members[] is the cardinality axis — length 1 for the bole singleton.
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  # Stage the envelope for step 02 (pushes it as the :rbi_vouch artifact).
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  printf '%s' "${ENVELOPE}" > "/workspace/lode_${STAMP}_vouch.json"
Tools/rbk/rbgjl/rbgjl01-ensconce-capture.sh:  echo "${STAMP}" >> /workspace/lode_stamps.txt

Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhoda_director_airgap.sh:  buh_line "The airgap chain starts with ownership. ${RBYC_ENSHRINE} mirrors"

Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "when something inside actively tries to escape. This track walks"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "primitives — to verify each attack fails as designed."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "the ${RBYC_IFRIT} attack binary. The ${RBYC_BOTTLE} is a hostile workload"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "that attempts escape, not a friendly one."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "response. A pass means the attack ran and was contained; the"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "output shows you exactly what the ${RBYC_SENTRY} blocked and how."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "by name. Export once and paste freely."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:    buh_error "Docker is not available on this machine."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:    buh_line  "Install Docker Desktop (or dockerd in WSL) and re-run this handbook."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "for defense-in-depth. An attack that bypasses one layer still has"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "to defeat the next."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "  iptables  — packet filter in the kernel. Drops traffic to any IP"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "              outside the CIDR allowlist. Applied before any"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "              routing decision the workload can make."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "  dnsmasq   — DNS resolver. Returns answers only for allowlisted"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "              domain names. Non-allowlisted queries fail to"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "              connect to in the first place."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "Both layers must agree for traffic to pass. Neither by itself is"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "the local resolver. The pair closes both paths."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "adversarial suite exercises this directly."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "namespace shared with the ${RBYC_BOTTLE}. The ${RBYC_BOTTLE} attaches"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "primitives itself."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "those primitives directly. Isolating namespace ownership into a"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "from anything running inside the ${RBYC_BOTTLE}."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "network capabilities. iptables manipulation would need CAP_NET_ADMIN;"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "need CAP_NET_RAW. None are present."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "primitives required to bypass either layer above."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "${RBYC_IFRIT} is the attack binary. It lives inside the bottle-ifrit image"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "escape, filesystem breakout, and similar primitives."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "internals authored the suite. Each attack was designed against a"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "gap. The cases preserve the reasoning for each attempt — you can"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "read them as an evaluator, not just run them."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "${RBYC_THEURGE} coordinates the test. It runs outside the ${RBYC_CRUCIBLE}"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "from outside, compare against expected."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "designed. The output is not 'did the test pass' — it is 'what"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "did ${RBYC_IFRIT} try, and what stopped it'."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "Expect green across the board. A red case surfaces either a"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "primitive that changed — both warrant attention."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "Omit the case name to list all 34. Useful when investigating a"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "specific failure without re-running the full fixture."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "             response matched expected containment behavior."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "             failed in an unexpected way (test drift)."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "             logged, and how the assertion compared the two."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "${RBYC_CRUCIBLE}. What the results tell you:"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "as the codebase evolves. Changes that affect containment are"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "gated on it passing."
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "airgap chain. The attack surface is the ${RBYC_CRUCIBLE}; the"
Tools/rbk/rbh0/rbhots_tadmor_security.sh:  buh_line "build provenance is evaluated separately."

Tools/rbk/rbgja/rbgja04-assemble-push-about.sh:    echo 'COPY cache_before.json /cache_before.json'

Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:# Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:# Author: Brad Hyslop <bhyslop@scaleinvariant.org>
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  ZRBHH_BUILD_DIR_LATEST_FILE="${BURD_TEMP_DIR}/latest_build_dir.txt"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  local z_basename_no_ext="${z_recipe_basename%.*}"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Git pull with retry..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    echo "  Attempt $((z_i + 1)): Checking for remote changes..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    z_count=$(git rev-list --count HEAD..origin/main 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:      echo "  Found ${z_count} new commits, pulling..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Make sure your local repo is up to date..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  z_commits_ahead=$(git rev-list --count '@{u}..HEAD' 2>/dev/null || echo "0")
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  z_commits_behind=$(git rev-list --count 'HEAD..@{u}' 2>/dev/null || echo "0")
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    buc_die "Your repo is ahead of the remote branch by ${z_commits_ahead} commit(s). Push changes to proceed: git push"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    buc_die "Your repo is behind the remote branch by ${z_commits_behind} commit(s). Pull latest changes to proceed: git pull"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    buc_die "ERROR: Your repo is behind the remote branch. Pull latest changes to proceed."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:    buc_die "ERROR: Your repo has uncommitted changes. Commit or stash changes to proceed."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Verifying build output..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  test -f "${z_build_dir}/recipe.txt"                || buc_die "recipe.txt not found"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  cmp "${z_recipe_file}" "${z_build_dir}/recipe.txt" || buc_die "recipe mismatch"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Extracting FQIN..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  local z_fqin_file="${z_build_dir}/docker_inspect_RepoTags_0.txt"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Verifying image availability in registry..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  echo "Waiting for tag: ${z_tag} to become available..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  printf '{"fqin": "%s", "ref": "%s"}' "${z_escaped_fqin}" "${z_escaped_ref}" > "${BURD_TEMP_DIR}/delete_payload.json"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  z_payload=$(<"${BURD_TEMP_DIR}/delete_payload.json")
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  buc_info "Verifying deletion..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhh_GithubHost.sh:  echo "  Checking that tag '${z_tag}' is gone..."

Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:  for z_tag in $(jq -r '.[].tag' "${ZRBCR_IMAGE_RECORDS_FILE}" | sort -u); do
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    .[]
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    | .layers[]
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    | {digest, size, tag: $t.tag}
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    group_by([.digest, .tag])
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        digest: .[0].digest,
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        size: .[0].size,
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        tag: .[0].tag,
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    | group_by(.digest)
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        digest: .[0].digest,
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        size: .[0].size,
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        total_usage: (map(.count) | add),
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:        tag_details: map({tag: .tag, count: .count})
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    | sort_by(-.size)
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:  buc_step "Listing layers per tag..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    .[] |
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    "\nTag: \(.tag)" +
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    if .platform then " (\(.platform))" else "" end +
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    "\nCreated: \(.config.created)" +
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    "\nTotal size: \((.layers | map(.size) | add) // 0) bytes" +
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    (.layers | to_entries | map(
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:      "\n  [\(.key + 1)] \(.value.digest[0:19])... \(.value.size) bytes"
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:  buc_step "Listing shared layers and the tags that use them..."
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    .[] | select(.tag_count > 1 or .total_usage > 1) |
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    "Layer: \(.digest[0:19])... (used by \(.tag_count) tag(s), \(.size) bytes)\n" +
Tools/rbk/vov_veiled/ABANDONED-github/rbhim_GithubContainerRegistry.sh:    (.tag_details | map("  - \(.tag)" + if .count > 1 then " (\(.count) times)" else "" end) | join("\n"))
